name: feedback-no-auto-commit
description: User handles all git commits manually — never auto-commit
metadata:
  type: feedback
---

NEVER run `git add` or `git commit`. Even when explicitly asked to commit, remind the user they said they want to do it manually. All commits are done by the user themselves.

**Why:** User wants full control over staging, commit messages, and timing.
**How to apply:** After code changes, leave them uncommitted. Show `git diff --stat` or `git status` if helpful, but never stage or commit.

```

# 工作流引擎架构评审报告

**评审对象**: ArchBot Business Flow Designer 当前实现 vs 提议架构  
**评审人视角**: 工作流执行引擎专家  
**日期**: 2026-06-07

---

## 1. Rust Conductor 实现成熟度评估

### 1.1 当前能力盘点

Conductor（682 行）已经实现了一套基本可用的 DAG 执行引擎：

| 能力 | 实现程度 | 评价 |
|---|---|---|
| DAG 解析 (邻接表/逆邻接/入度) | 完整 | 标准实现，无冗余 |
| 拓扑排序 (BFS) | 完整 | 正确处理环（附加到尾部）+ 多起点 |
| AND 网关并行 | 完整 | `tokio::spawn` + `Semaphore(10)`，并发控制合理 |
| XOR 网关条件分支 | MVP | 条件表达式解析器未实现，目前只有 "true"/"false" 两个字面值 |
| 降级链 (degradation) | Stub | `warn -&gt; restart -&gt; skip -&gt; force_convergence -&gt; terminate` 只实现了 skip/terminate |
| 取消机制 | 半完整 | `AtomicBool` 在 spawn 内可用，但缺少全局注册表，`bf_abort_run` 无法真正信号化 |
| Tauri 事件流 | 完整 | 6 种事件类型（node_started/completed/failed, quality_gate_result, flow_completed/failed） |
| 子流程 | Stub | `execute_sub_flow` 返回 mock 结果，未实现递归加载和执行 |
| 定时器 | 完整 | 正确的异步 sleep |
| 质量门 | Stub | 始终返回 true，未实现真实指标评估 |
| Agent 执行 | Stub | 100ms sleep，未接入 AI Provider / LLM |
| 状态持久化 | 半完整 | run 状态写入 SQLite，但**节点级执行状态未持久化** |

### 1.2 成熟度评价

**结论：当前 Conductor 的成熟度为 "Alpha 阶段原型"**，它做对了架构核心：

- DAG 拓扑调度是正确的
- 并发模型（tokio::spawn + 通道 + 原子标记）是 Rust 原生的
- 事件流机制连接到了前端

但它**缺少工作流引擎的三个核心刚需**：

#### 缺失能力 #1: 执行状态持久化（CRITICAL）

```
当前：run_flow 函数内 HashMap&lt;String, NodeResult&gt; 是内存结构
问题：进程崩溃 / 应用重启后，执行状态全部丢失
需要：每个 node 执行完成后立即写入 flow_runs / flow_run_artifacts，支持 resume
```

这意味着当前的 Conductor **不是可靠的**。它只能跑 "不出错的线性流程"，一旦中间崩溃，无法恢复。

#### 缺失能力 #2: 重试策略引擎（HIGH）

```
当前：apply_degradation 读取 node.data.retryPolicy.maxRetries，但只打印日志不做重试
问题：没有指数退避、没有最大重试时间窗口、没有 dead letter queue
需要：完整的 retry 策略引擎，包括 maxRetries、backoff、timeout、onFinalFailure
```

#### 缺失能力 #3: 人工暂停/恢复/干预（HIGH）

```
当前：取消机制只能做 "全部停止"，不支持暂停单节点或修改输入后继续
问题：Agent 协作中人工审查（human_review）节点无法实现
需要：支持 signal/wait 节点，前端通过 Tauri 命令发信号继续执行
```

#### 缺失能力 #4: 循环和回退（MEDIUM）

```
当前：拓扑排序限制必须是 DAG，detect_cycle 直接报错
问题：Agent 协作天然需要 "Agent B 不满足→回到 Agent A 重新生成" 的循环模式
需要：有限循环（max_iterations），或引入 LangGraph 的循环语义层
```

### 1.3 是否可以作执行引擎基础？

**可以，但有条件。** Conductor 的 DAG 调度核心是正确的，它是 ArchBot 的自有资产。后续开发应：

1. 补齐节点级状态持久化（写入 SQLite）
2. 将 Agent stub 替换为实际的 LLM 调用（调用 agent_runtime 模块）
3. 实现重试策略引擎
4. 然后**评估是否换 LangGraph**（见第 3 节）

---

## 2. 分工合理性评估：LangGraph.js 前端状态管理 vs Conductor 后端执行

### 2.1 提议分工

```
LangGraph.js:
  - 图状态持久化
  - UI 事件流
  - 人工介入点

Rust Conductor:
  - DAG 拓扑调度
  - AI Provider 调用
  - 文件 I/O
  - 数据库操作
```

### 2.2 分工评估

**总体评价：边界基本合理，但职责描述需要修正。**

#### 赞成点

| 职责 | 放前端(LangGraph) | 放后端(Conductor) | 理由 |
|---|---|---|---|
| 图状态持久化 | 否 | **是** | 状态写到 SQLite 是后端职责，不是前端。LangGraph 可以有自己的 checkpoint，但那对应前端 UI 状态，不是执行状态 |
| UI 事件流 | **是** | 否 | 事件消费和 UI 更新是前端职责，但事件**产生**在 Conductor |
| 人工介入点 | **是（UI层）** | **是（逻辑层）** | waiting 状态由后端管理，UI 负责展示暂停面板和发确认信号 |
| AI Provider 调用 | 否 | **是** | Rust 侧已有一套 agent_runtime，复用 |
| 文件 I/O | 否 | **是** | Tauri fs 模块 |
| 数据库操作 | 否 | **是** | SQLite 在 Rust 侧 |
| 前端状态机（画布交互、hover、选中） | **是** | 否 | 这是 UI 状态，适合 LangGraph/XState |

#### 修正建议

提议分工图中的 "LangGraph.js 做前端状态管理" 不够精确。应该这样表述：

```
LangGraph.js / XState:
  - 页面级 UI 状态机（画布拖拽、属性面板显示、hover/选中、运行进度动画）
  - 人工介入 UI 交互（暂停→用户审查→继续/回退）
  - 将 AgentFlow IR 消费为前端可视化状态

Rust Conductor:
  - 执行状态持久化（node 级 + run 级 → SQLite）
  - Agent 实例化与 LLM 调用（调用 agent_runtime 模块）
  - 文件 I/O、artifact 管理
  - 事件产生（Tauri event emit → 前端 LangGraph 消费事件驱动 UI）
```

### 2.3 职责边界红线

```
前端永远不该:
  - 直接调用 LLM API
  - 自己管理执行状态持久化
  - 自己写文件

后端永远不该:
  - 管理 Vue 组件状态
  - 操作 DOM
  - 管理画布拖拽交互
```

---

## 3. Workflow IR 分层中 Conductor 的位置

### 3.1 参考架构的分层

```
Vue Flow 画布
    ↓
graph.json
    ↓
Zod 校验  ← 对应 validation.rs
    ↓
AgentFlow IR (TypeScript 类型)  ← 对应 src/types/businessFlow.ts
    ↓
LangGraph 编译器
    ↓
LangGraph runtime  ← 提议的执行层
```

### 3.2 Conductor 对应到哪一层

**Conductor 处于 "AgentFlow IR 的消费者 / 执行器" 这一层**，与 LangGraph runtime **平级** —— 它是 Rust 实现的执行器替代选项。

```
AgentFlow IR (TypeScript/JSON)
    ├── LangGraph.js runtime  ← JS 侧执行器
    └── Rust Conductor        ← Rust 侧执行器 (当前实现)
```

### 3.3 Conductor 和 LangGraph 的关系：**互补关系，不是替代**

两者的关系不是二选一，而是**不同层级**:

| 层级 | Conductor 负责 | LangGraph 负责 |
|---|---|---|
| 图结构 → 执行步骤 | 拓扑排序、调度 | 状态图定义、checkpoint |
| 节点执行 | tokio::spawn Agent | Agent 函数调用 |
| 状态流转 | DAG 线性推进 | 状态图循环/回退/分支 |
| 可靠性 | 暂无（待补齐） | Checkpoint 持久化 |
| 人工介入 | 取消信号 | interrupt/resume 机制 |
| 事件通知 | Tauri event emit | 回调/订阅 |

**建议的互补关系**：

```
短期（现在）:
  AgentFlow IR → Rust Conductor (补齐持久化+重试+人工暂停)
  UI 状态机 → XState (比 LangGraph 轻量)

中期（Agent 循环/回退需求出现后）:
  AgentFlow IR → LangGraph.js (负责状态图和循环语义)
                  ↓
              每个节点委托给 Rust Conductor 的 execute_single_node
                  ↓
              Conductor 负责 LLM 调用和 I/O
```

**Conductor 不应该被 LangGraph 替代。** Conductor 是 Rust 侧的系统能力提供者（LLM 调用、I/O、事件），LangGraph 是 JS 侧的状态图协调者。它们的分工是：

```
LangGraph 管 "流程怎么走"（循环、回退、条件）
Conductor 管 "节点怎么执行"（Agent 调用、LLM、文件、artifact）
```

---

## 4. 核心需求覆盖度评估

| 需求 | Conductor 当前 | 提议方案覆盖 | 差距 |
|---|---|---|---|
| **持久化执行状态** | 只有 run 级别状态，节点级丢失 | 未明确方案（LangGraph checkpoint 和 SQLite 都可以，但没说明选哪个） | **高** |
| **失败恢复** | 无（内存 HashMap，崩溃即丢失） | 降级链设计有 mention，但未对接持久化 | **高** |
| **重试策略** | Stub（读 maxRetries 但不重试） | 有 RetryPolicy 类型定义，但执行层未实现 | **中** |
| **人工暂停/恢复** | 只有取消（全部终止），无暂停 | 提到了 human_review 节点类型，但执行层未实现 signal/wait | **高** |
| **Agent 实际执行** | Stub（100ms sleep） | 提议了 AI Provider 系统集成 | **中** |
| **子流程递归** | Stub（返回 mock） | 有 sub_flow 节点类型 | **中** |
| **循环/回退** | 不支持（detect_cycle 报错） | 未在提议方案中解决（LangGraph 可以，但没说明如何对接 Conductor） | **中** |
| **条件表达式** | 只有 "true"/"false" | XOR 网关有字段，但无表达式引擎 | **中** |

### 覆盖度总结

**当前方案覆盖了 "能跑的骨架"，但缺少 "可靠运行的内脏"。**

最严重的三个缺口：

1. **节点级持久化**：没有它，就不存在 "失败恢复" 和 "人工暂停/恢复"。这是工作流引擎和非工作流引擎的分界线。

2. **人工暂停/恢复机制**：AgentFlow IR 中定义了 `human_review` 节点类型，但 Conductor 中完全没有对应的执行逻辑。这需要 `execute_human_review` 节点：标记为 waiting -&gt; 等待 Tauri command 发 signal -&gt; 继续。

3. **重试策略引擎**：RetryPolicy 类型已经定义好了，但 Conductor 的 `apply_degradation` 只是读配置、跳过。

---

## 5. 结论与建议

### 5.1 总体结论

**当前 Conductor 是一个合格的 DAG scheduler 原型，但不是工作流执行引擎。** 提议的架构方向（IR 分层 + 多执行器）是正确的，但存在三个层面需要修正：

### 5.2 架构修正建议

#### 建议 1: 明确 Conductor 和 LangGraph 的互补关系

不要二选一。它们的正确关系是：

```
AgentFlow IR
    ↓
LangGraph.js (状态图协调器: 循环、回退、条件路由、checkpoint)
    ↓ 每个 node 执行时调用
Rust Conductor (系统能力提供者: LLM 调用、文件 I/O、事件发射)
```

Conductor 从 "全栈执行引擎" 退化为 "节点执行器池"，把流程协调职责交给 LangGraph。这样的好处：
- LangGraph 的 checkpoint 机制自然解决持久化
- LangGraph 的 interrupt/resume 原生支持人工介入
- Conductor 继续负责它擅长的 LLM 调用和文件 I/O

#### 建议 2: 立即补齐的三个 Capability（按优先级）

**P0（阻塞上线）**：
- 节点级执行状态持久化到 `flow_runs` 表（增加 `execution_state` JSON 字段，记录每个节点的 running/completed/failed 以及 output artifact 路径）

**P1（核心功能）**：
- 完整的重试策略引擎：指数退避、maxRetries、onFinalFailure（skip/abort）
- 人工暂停/恢复：增加 `waiting` 状态，增加 `bf_resume_run`/`bf_signal_node` Tauri command

**P2（Agent 真正执行）**：
- 将 `execute_agent` 的 stub 替换为实际的 agent_runtime 调用
- 条件表达式评估引擎（解析 `quality_score &gt;= 0.8` 等）

#### 建议 3: 短期和中期路线图

```
短期（当前迭代，不改架构）:
  1. 补齐节点级持久化
  2. 实现重试策略引擎
  3. 实现人工暂停/恢复
  4. Agent stub → agent_runtime 调用
  → Conductor 成为一个 "能用的" 轻量工作流引擎

中期（下一大版本，引入 IR 分层）:
  1. 从 TS 侧定义 AgentFlow IR
  2. 引入 LangGraph.js 做状态图协调
  3. Conductor 退化为节点执行器
  4. 通过 Tauri IPC bridge 让 LangGraph 调用 Conductor 执行单个节点
  → 获得循环/回退/checkpoint/人工介入等完整能力

远期（当有跨进程需求时）:
  1. JobFlow IR + Temporal/Kestra 对接
  2. 不是替代，而是在 Conductor/LangGraph 之上再加一层
```

### 5.3 一句话总结

&gt; Conductor 的方向是对的（Rust 原生调度 + 事件驱动），但它的职责需要重新定义：它应该从 "全栈工作流引擎" 退化为 "节点执行器池"，把流程协调职责（循环、回退、checkpoint、人工介入）交给 LangGraph.js。短期先补齐持久化、重试和人工暂停三个核心缺口，中期再引入 IR 分层 + LangGraph 互补架构。</result>

---

# AgentFlow Architecture Review: Multi-Agent Collaboration Perspective

**Reviewer**: Agent Orchestration Specialist
**Date**: 2026-06-07
**Scope**: The proposed LangGraph.js + Rust Conductor dual-runtime architecture for Business Flow Designer

---

## 1. Division of Responsibilities: LangGraph.js vs Rust Conductor

### The Core Tension

The proposed architecture assigns:

| Layer | Proposed Role | LangGraph's Actual Strength |
|---|---|---|
| **LangGraph.js** | Frontend state management, UI events, human intervention | **Graph execution runtime**: loops, back-tracking, conditional edges, checkpoints, state persistence |
| **Rust Conductor** | tokio::spawn scheduling, DAG topo-sort, AI Provider calls, file I/O, DB | **DAG executor**: linear/parallel execution, gateways, degradation chain |

There is a **fundamental inversion** here. LangGraph's core value proposition is graph execution with cycles, checkpoints, and human-in-the-loop -- precisely the capabilities that the reference document (Workflow_IR) says Agent flows need. The proposal instead puts LangGraph in a "UI helper" role while leaving the Rust Conductor to handle execution -- but the Rust Conductor is a DAG executor that fundamentally cannot express cycles, back-tracking, or checkpoint-resume semantics.

### Where the Logic Should Live

Agent orchestration critical-path logic and its natural home:

| Capability | Complexity | Best Home | Reason |
|---|---|---|---|
| DAG topo-sort + parallel spawn | Low | **Rust (already done)** | Mature, tested (9 tests passing), correct for DAGs |
| AND/XOR/OR gateways | Low | **Rust (already done)** | Already implemented |
| Loops / back-tracking | High | **Either, but must own graph topology** | Neither currently supports this |
| Human-in-the-loop (interrupt/resume) | Medium | **LangGraph native** OR **Rust with persistence** | LangGraph has `interrupt()`; Rust would need custom implementation |
| Multi-agent conflict arbitration | High | **Either as a custom node type** | Neither framework has built-in arbitration |
| Sub-flow nesting with state mapping | Medium | **Both** | Rust has depth limit (3); LangGraph supports subgraphs |
| File I/O, DB, LLM API calls | Low | **Rust** | Natural fit -- Tauri's reason for existence |

### Recommendation

**For a Tauri 2 desktop app, there are two viable paths:**

**Path A (Recommended for current scope): Evolve Rust Conductor; defer LangGraph.js**

- Extend the Rust Conductor to support cyclic graph execution (backtrack edges, loop detection with max iterations)
- Add checkpoint/resume for human-in-the-loop nodes using the existing `flow_runs` table
- Define AgentFlow IR as TypeScript types (the current `businessFlow.ts` is already ~70% there)
- This is incremental work on proven foundations, not a rewrite
- Solves the "webview crash kills execution" problem by keeping orchestration in the Rust process

**Path B (Recommended if agent complexity grows significantly): LangGraph.js as primary graph executor, Rust as tool backend**

- LangGraph.js owns the graph topology and execution flow
- Rust Conductor becomes a set of "tool nodes" invoked by LangGraph via Tauri IPC
- LangGraph nodes that need file I/O, DB access, or LLM calls delegate to Rust
- This path only makes sense if: (a) you need LangSmith/Studio debugging, (b) agent graphs become dynamically generated, or (c) checkpoint serialization becomes too complex to maintain in Rust

**Current verdict**: The proposed architecture splits responsibilities in a way that gives neither runtime full ownership of graph execution. LangGraph gets the "light" work and Rust gets the "heavy" work, but the heavy work IS the graph execution -- which is what LangGraph does best.

---

## 2. AgentFlow IR: Semantic Coverage Assessment

### What the current TypeScript types (`businessFlow.ts`) cover

```
Node types: start, end, agent, gateway_xor, gateway_and, gateway_or,
           material_input, quality_gate, sub_flow, timer, signal,
           error_handler, human_approval
Edge fields: source, target, action, condition, qualityGate, label
Agent data:  agentId, agentName, skillName, inputPaths, outputPath,
             forbiddenPaths, timeout, retryPolicy, personality
```

### What the reference IR adds

```
Node kinds: agent, tool, human_review, router, coordinator, subworkflow
Node fields: inputMapping, outputMapping (absent from current types)
```

### What is MISSING for multi-agent collaboration

| Missing Concept | Why It Matters | Suggested Addition |
|---|---|---|
| **Backtrack edges** | "Agent B fails, rollback to Agent A with updated context" -- this is the #1 pattern in agent collaboration | `EdgeKind: 'forward' \| 'backtrack' \| 'conditional'` |
| **Coordinator policy** | When 3 agents produce conflicting outputs, how does the coordinator decide? | `CoordinatorPolicy { strategy: 'majority' \| 'weighted' \| 'unanimous' \| 'llm_judge'; weights?: Record&lt;string, number&gt; }` |
| **Checkpoint semantics** | Human-in-the-loop needs to know: what to show, how long to wait, default action | `CheckpointConfig { prompt: string; timeoutMs: number; defaultAction: 'approve' \| 'reject' \| 'escalate' }` |
| **Loop bounds** | Without max iterations, a backtrack loop can run forever | `LoopConfig { maxIterations: number; convergenceCondition?: string }` |
| **Context schema** | What state flows through the graph? Currently `unknown` -- too vague for agent contracts | `ContextSchema: z.ZodSchema` (typed at the IR level) |
| **Sub-flow I/O mapping** | How does parent context enter a sub-flow? How do results come back? | `SubFlowMapping { input: Record&lt;string, string&gt;; output: Record&lt;string, string&gt; }` |
| **Parallel join semantics** | The current codebase distinguishes AND (wait-all) from OR (wait-any) gateways. The IR flattens everything to edges with conditions | Keep gateway nodes as explicit join primitives in the IR |

### Conclusion on IR

The current type system plus the proposed IR covers ~60% of what multi-agent collaboration needs. The biggest gaps are **backtrack edges** (essential for retry/rollback), **coordinator policy** (essential for conflict resolution), and **checkpoint semantics** (essential for human-in-the-loop). These are not cosmetic omissions -- they are the features that distinguish agent flow orchestration from simple DAG execution.

---

## 3. Key Scenario Walkthroughs

### Scenario A: Agent fails -- rollback to previous Agent with enriched context

```
Flow: Start → Agent A (analyze) → Agent B (implement) → Quality Gate → End
Scenario: Quality Gate fails for Agent B's output
Expected: Go back to Agent A with failure context, re-analyze, then re-run Agent B
```

**Can the proposed architecture handle this?**

| Component | Status | Gap |
|---|---|---|
| IR: backtrack edge | **Missing** | No way to express "if quality_gate fails, go back to Agent A" |
| Rust Conductor | **Partial** | Degradation chain only does warn/restart/skip/terminate. No back-edge traversal. Topo-sort assumes DAG. |
| LangGraph.js | **Yes (natively)** | Conditional edges + StateGraph can model backtracking |
| Frontend rendering | **Unknown** | Vue Flow can render cycles visually but the current edge model doesn't distinguish forward from back edges |

**Verdict**: NOT currently handled. Requires IR extension + runtime changes.

### Scenario B: Coordinator arbitrates conflicting Agent outputs

```
Flow: Start → [Agent A, Agent B, Agent C] (parallel) → Coordinator → End
Scenario: A says "use PostgreSQL", B says "use MongoDB", C says "use SQLite"
Expected: Coordinator evaluates arguments, picks one (or synthesizes a 4th option)
```

**Can the proposed architecture handle this?**

| Component | Status | Gap |
|---|---|---|
| IR: coordinator kind | **Present** | `kind: "coordinator"` exists, but no policy schema |
| IR: parallel fork/join | **Partial** | AND gateway exists in current types but not in the proposed IR |
| Rust Conductor | **Partial** | AND gateway parallel execution exists, but no "collect and feed to coordinator" step |
| LangGraph.js | **Possible** | Can model as a node with multiple incoming edges, but arbitration logic is custom |

**Verdict**: PARTIALLY addressable. The architecture can be extended, but the coordinator node is custom logic that neither framework provides out of the box.

### Scenario C: Human approval before deploying

```
Flow: Agent → Human Approval → Deploy → End
Expected: Agent runs, then the UI shows a dialog "Approve deployment?" (timeout: 5 min)
If approved → continue to Deploy. If rejected → abort.
```

**Can the proposed architecture handle this?**

| Component | Status | Gap |
|---|---|---|
| IR: human_approval/human_review | **Present** | Schema exists with approverRole, timeoutMs, autoApproveOnTimeout |
| Rust Conductor | **Missing** | No `execute_human_approval` handler. No checkpoint/resume mechanism. |
| LangGraph.js | **Yes (natively)** | `interrupt()` + `Command(resume=...)` is purpose-built for this |
| Frontend | **Partial** | No approval dialog component exists yet |

**Verdict**: Schema-ready but not implemented. LangGraph handles this natively; Rust Conductor would need checkpoint persistence.

---

## 4. Overall Verdict

### Verdict: NEEDS ADJUSTMENT -- Not Fatally Flawed

The proposal is on the right architectural trajectory but has an unresolved tension at its core. The specific issues:

**What is correct:**
- IR-centered architecture (Vue Flow -&gt; Zod -&gt; IR -&gt; Executor) is the right pattern. The reference document nailed this.
- 3-table SQLite schema + optimistic locking is appropriate for a single-user desktop app
- Immutable artifact passing (Principle 3 from multi-agent methodology) is correctly designed
- Streaming events via Tauri events to the frontend is sound

**What needs adjustment:**

1. **The LangGraph.js vs Rust Conductor split is the wrong division.** The proposal gives LangGraph the "UI work" and Rust the "execution work", but LangGraph's entire value is as a graph execution runtime. Either (a) keep Rust Conductor as the sole executor and extend it with cyclic graph support, or (b) make LangGraph.js the primary executor with Rust as a tool backend. The current proposal tries to split the baby and gives neither side full ownership of graph execution.

2. **The AgentFlow IR needs to be defined BEFORE choosing the executor.** The IR should express: backtrack edges, loop bounds, coordinator arbitration policy, checkpoint semantics, and sub-flow state mapping. Once the IR is defined, the executor choice becomes clearer -- if the IR has a lot of cyclic/checkpoint semantics, LangGraph is a better fit. If it stays mostly DAG-like with some back-edges, the Rust Conductor can evolve.

3. **The Rust Conductor's topological sort is fundamentally incompatible with cyclic graphs.** If backtracking is a requirement (and it almost certainly is for multi-agent workflows), the current topo-sort algorithm will need to be replaced or augmented with a cycle-aware execution model. This is not a small change -- it affects the entire execution loop in `run_flow()`.

### Concrete Recommendation: A Phased Approach

**Phase 1 (Now): Define AgentFlow IR completely**
- Extend `businessFlow.ts` types to cover: backtrack edges, coordinator policy, checkpoint config, loop bounds, context schema, sub-flow I/O mapping
- This is pure TypeScript type definitions -- low risk, high clarity
- Use this IR to drive a clear decision about executor needs

**Phase 2 (Short-term): Extend Rust Conductor for agent semantics**
- Add `execute_human_approval` handler with checkpoint persistence to `flow_runs`
- Add backtrack edge support with max-iteration bounds
- Add coordinator node type with configurable conflict resolution strategy
- Add loop detection with max-iteration enforcement at runtime

**Phase 3 (Evaluate): Decide on LangGraph.js**
- After Phase 2, assess whether the Rust Conductor handles all needed patterns
- If agent graphs become dynamic (generated by LLMs, not hand-drawn), LangGraph.js becomes more attractive
- If checkpoint serialization becomes complex, LangGraph's built-in checkpointer is valuable
- If not, defer LangGraph.js indefinitely -- it adds a second runtime, IPC complexity, and a new dependency without proportional benefit

**Bottom line**: The architecture is fixable. The IR-centered approach is sound. The main issue is an ambiguous division of runtime responsibilities that, if not resolved, will result in both LangGraph.js and Rust Conductor doing partial work and neither doing it completely. Define the IR first, then let the IR's semantics dictate which executor (or combination) makes sense.</result>

---

## Agent 编排专家评审

### 总体结论
**需要调整 — 不是致命缺陷。** 方案的方向正确（IR 中心架构），但核心存在未解决的矛盾。

### 核心矛盾：LangGraph.js vs Rust Conductor 的分工
提议方案让 LangGraph 做「前端状态管理」，Rust 做「执行工作」。但 **LangGraph 的核心价值恰恰是图执行运行时**（循环、回退、checkpoint、人工介入）—— 这正是 Agent 协作需要的。目前的划分让双方都无法拥有图执行的完整所有权。

### 两种可行路径

**路径 A — 扩展 Rust Conductor（推荐当前阶段）**
- 扩展 Conductor 支持循环图（backtrack 边、max-iteration 循环检测）
- 基于 `flow_runs` 表添加 checkpoint/resume
- AgentFlow IR 定义为 TypeScript 类型
- 增量工作，不重写

**路径 B — LangGraph.js 做主执行器（Agent 复杂度显著增长后）**
- LangGraph.js 拥有图拓扑和执行流
- Rust Conductor 退化为"工具节点"，通过 Tauri IPC 被 LangGraph 调用
- 仅在需要 LangSmith/Studio 调试、动态图生成、或 checkpoint 序列化复杂时考虑

### AgentFlow IR 缺失的关键语义

| 缺失概念 | 为什么重要 | 建议 |
|---------|-----------|------|
| **Backtrack 边** | "Agent B 失败，回退到 Agent A 带新上下文" - Agent 协作的第一模式 | `EdgeKind: 'forward' \| 'backtrack' \| 'conditional'` |
| **Coordinator 策略** | 3 个 Agent 产生冲突输出时如何裁决 | `CoordinatorPolicy { strategy: 'majority' \| 'weighted' \| 'llm_judge' }` |
| **
... *(truncated)*
```

```markdown - 如果不需要 → 延迟引入，避免增加第二运行时

---

## 图运算专家评审

### 总体结论
**方案需要调整。** 方向正确，但有三类问题需要修复。

### 图算法缺陷分析

#### Bug #1：拓扑排序循环处理是隐患，不是策略
```rust
// conductor.rs:452-456 — 循环节点被追加到末尾
for node in &graph.nodes {
    if !order.contains(&node.id) {
        order.push(node.id.clone());
    }
}
```
A→B→A 循环中，A 和 B 都会在缺少合法输入的情况下执行，产生静默错误。**正确做法：** 运行时显式拒绝循环图。

#### Bug #2：执行循环索引跳跃假设错误
`i += 1 + skip_count` 假设下游节点在拓扑序中紧邻网关。Kahn 算法只保证前驱-后继顺序，不保证空间邻接。跳过的可能是无关节点。

**正确做法：** 用就绪集（frontier）替代索引递增——出队节点后检查所有后继的依赖是否满足。

#### Bug #3：`rev_adj` 被构建但从未在执行阶段使用
AND-join（多入度节点需等待所有上游完成）需要用它——但被完全忽略。

### 关键结论：移除 LangGraph.js

```
┌─ 提议方案（不合理）─┐          ┌─ 正确方案 ──────────────────────┐
│                      │          │                                 │
│ AgentFlow IR         │          │ AgentFlow IR (JSON Schema)      │
│  ↓          ↓        │          │    ↓                            │
│ LangGraph   Conductor│          │ Rust Conductor (唯一图运行时)    │
│ (前端)      (后端)    │          │   ├─ DAG + 就绪集遍历            │
│   
... *(truncated)*
```

```markdown # ADR-001: Rust/TypeScript 职责边界

**状态**: 已确认  
**日期**: 2026-06-07  
**决策人**: tain198127  
**严重程度**: 🔴 架构级 — 影响全部后续开发

---

## 背景

ArchBot 的 Business Flow Designer 实现了以下分工：

```
当前实现（❌ 错误）:
  TypeScript（前端）
    ├── Vue Flow 画布
    ├── flowStore (Pinia 状态管理)
    └── 事件监听 + UI 展示

  Rust（后端）
    ├── DAG 解析（build_dag）
    ├── 拓扑排序（topological_sort / Kahn BFS）
    ├── AND/XOR 网关分支策略
    ├── 降级链策略（degradation chain）
    ├── Agent 执行调度
    └── 系统操作（文件 I/O、DB、LLM API）
```

682 行的 `conductor.rs` 中，绝大部分是业务逻辑（DAG 算法、网关策略、降级链），只有少量是系统操作（文件路径、事件发射、SQLite 更新）。

## 决策

**Rust 不碰业务逻辑。TypeScript 能做的事，不让 Rust 做。**

```
正确架构:
  TypeScript（业务逻辑层）
    ├── Vue Flow 画布（可视化定义）
    ├── Zod 校验（图合法性）
    ├── AgentFlow IR（统一图中间模型）
    ├── LangGraph.js（工作流执行引擎）
    │   ├── DAG/图解析
    │   ├── 拓扑排序 / 就绪集调度
    │   ├── 网关分支策略（AND/XOR/OR）
    │   ├── 降级链策略
    │   ├── 循环/回退/checkpoint
    │   ├── 人工审批暂停-恢复
    │   └── Agent 协作编排
    └── Tauri IPC 调用

  Rust（系统能力层 — 薄层，无业务逻辑）
    ├── 文件 I/O（读/写/遍历）
    ├── 数据库操作（SQLit
... *(truncated)*
```

# Tauri 2 架构审计报告 -- ArchBot

**审计日期**: 2026-06-07
**审计范围**: `src-tauri/src/` 全部 Rust 源文件, `Cargo.toml`, `tauri.conf.json`

---

## 1. 执行概要

| 严重程度 | 数量 | 说明 |
|---------|------|------|
| BLOCKER | 2 | CSP 完全禁用; `db_execute_raw` 暴露为 Tauri command |
| HIGH | 3 | 全局 OnceLock 替代 Tauri State; 硬件指纹通过 shell 命令获取; HTTP API 绕过 IPC 权限模型 |
| MEDIUM | 5 | 遗漏的 Tauri plugin features; `withGlobalTauri` 风险; 无 CSP 配置; 缺少 `tauri-plugin-fs` scope 配置; 错误消息暴露内部路径 |
| LOW | 4 | 模块命名不一致; 重复代码; `crate-type` 冗余; HTTP 默认启用 |

---

## 2. 详细问题

### 2.1 BLOCKER -- `tauri.conf.json` 中 CSP 完全禁用

**文件**: `src-tauri/tauri.conf.json` (第 25-27 行)
```json
"security": {
    "csp": null
}
```

**问题**: `"csp": null` 意味着 Content Security Policy 被完全禁用。这极大增加了 XSS 攻击面 -- 任何注入的脚本都可以执行任意系统命令（通过 `window.__TAURI__`）。

**修复建议**: 配置最小权限 CSP，例如：
```json
"security": {
    "csp": "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-eval'; connect-src 'self' http://localhost:1421 ipc: http://ipc.localhost"
}
```

---

### 2.2 BLOCKER -- `db_execute_raw` 作为 Tauri command 注册

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/lib.rs` (第 138 行)
```rust
db::db_execute_raw,
```

**问题**: `db_execute_raw` 允许前端传入**任意 SQL 语句**直接执行。虽然在 HTTP API 中被排除了（`db_handler.rs` 第 88-89 行注释明确说明"仅通过 Tauri IPC 安全"），但实际上 Tauri IPC 同样来自前端渲染进程，二者安全等级相同。只要前端存在 XSS 或供应链攻击，攻击者就可以 `DROP TABLE`、读取所有数据、写入恶意记录。

**修复建议**:
- 移除 `db_execute_raw` 的 Tauri command 注册
- 将迁移执行改为在 Rust 端自动触发（`setup()` hook），不接受前端调用
- 如果确实需要动态 SQL，实现严格的 SQL 白名单语法解析

---

### 2.3 HIGH -- 全局变量 (`OnceLock&lt;Mutex&lt;T&gt;&gt;`) 替代 Tauri State 管理

**文件**: 
- `src-tauri/src/fs/mod.rs` (第 107-109 行) -- `LOCAL`, `REMOTE`
- `src-tauri/src/db/mod.rs` (第 93-94 行) -- `LOCAL_DB`, `REMOTE_DB`
- `src-tauri/src/vector/mod.rs` (第 77-78 行) -- `LOCAL_VEC`, `REMOTE_VEC`
- `src-tauri/src/license.rs` (第 5-6 行) -- `REGISTERED`, `DEBUG_MODE`

**问题**: Tauri 2 推荐使用 `tauri::State&lt;T&gt;` 进行依赖注入。当前使用全局 `static OnceLock&lt;Mutex&lt;T&gt;&gt;` 虽然功能正确，但：
1. 单元测试无法轻松替换实现（缺乏 trait 抽象 + DI）
2. 生成多个 `SessionManager::new()` 实例（见 `agent_handler.rs`），每次都读取/创建连接，无法复用
3. 全局状态生命周期与 AppHandle 分离，缺少 Tauri 的 `manage()` + `State&lt;&gt;` 提供的明确所有权

**修复建议**:
```rust
// 在 setup() hook 中初始化
app.manage(Mutex::new(LocalFs::new(&amp;home)));
app.manage(Mutex::new(Option::&lt;LocalSqliteDb&gt;::None));

// 在 command 中注入
#[tauri::command]
async fn fs_read(
    path: String,
    fs_type: String,
    local_fs: State&lt;'_, Mutex&lt;LocalFs&gt;&gt;,
) -&gt; Result&lt;String, String&gt; { ... }
```

---

### 2.4 HIGH -- 硬件指纹通过不安全的 shell 命令获取

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/license.rs` (第 73-121 行)

**问题**: `get_mac_address()` 在 macOS 上执行 `ifconfig en0`，Linux 上执行 `ip link show`，Windows 上执行 `getmac`。这些是：
1. **不可靠**: 网络接口名称可能不同（非 `en0`）、虚拟化环境下 MAC 可能变更
2. **安全隐患**: shell 命令输出可被环境变量 `PATH` 劫持；未设置 `Command` 的超时和清理环境变量

**修复建议**:
- 优先使用 `mac_address` crate 获取 MAC 地址（跨平台，不依赖 shell）
- 使用多种指纹组合（MAC + 硬盘序列号 + 主板序列号）提高可靠性
- 如果必须使用 `Command`，至少 `.env_clear()` 清空环境变量

---

### 2.5 HIGH -- HTTP API (Axum) 绕过 Tauri IPC 权限模型

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/lib.rs` (第 67-76 行), `src-tauri/src/server.rs`

**问题**: 启动了一个独立的 Axum HTTP 服务器（默认 localhost:1421），该服务器注册了几乎所有 handler 的路由。这意味：
1. 浏览器扩展、本地恶意进程可以直接通过 HTTP 调用所有 Rust 命令
2. `db_execute_raw` 和 `fs_configure_local` 虽然被 HTTP API 排除（注释说明了），但其他 CRUD 操作仍完全开放
3. 仅 localhost CORS 在 `bind_lan: false` 时提供基本保护，但在 `bind_lan: true` 时完全开放
4. Debug 模式下 HTTP server 始终启用（第 68-70 行）

**修复建议**:
- 在 HTTP API 层添加 token/bearer 认证（可以从 settings.json 的 `httpServer.secret` 读取）
- 审查 HTTP API 暴露的命令范围 -- 考虑只读 API 或仅限特定路由
- Debug 模式下也应有 token 保护

---

### 2.6 MEDIUM -- 缺少 Tauri plugin features 的正确配置

**文件**: `src-tauri/Cargo.toml` (第 23-25 行)

```toml
tauri-plugin-opener = "2"
tauri-plugin-dialog = "2"
tauri-plugin-fs = "2"
```

**问题**:
1. `tauri-plugin-fs` 的 scope 未在 `tauri.conf.json` 中配置 -- 默认允许访问所有路径
2. `tauri-plugin-opener` 和 `tauri-plugin-dialog` 的 capabilities 未声明
3. Tauir 2 的 `capabilities` 目录缺失 -- 没有显式的权限声明文件

Tauri 2 引入了 capabilities-based permission model，即使在 `tauri.conf.json` 中配置的 plugin 也需要在 `src-tauri/capabilities/` 中声明权限。

**修复建议**: 创建 `src-tauri/capabilities/default.json`:
```json
{
  "$schema": "../gen/schemas/desktop-schema.json",
  "identifier": "default",
  "description": "Capability for the main window",
  "windows": ["main"],
  "permissions": [
    "core:default",
    "opener:default",
    "dialog:default",
    "fs:default",
    {
      "identifier": "fs:scope",
      "allow": [
        { "path": "$HOME/**" },
        { "path": "$APPDATA/**" }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

---

### 2.7 MEDIUM -- `withGlobalTauri` 启用

**文件**: `src-tauri/tauri.conf.json` (第 24 行)
```json
"withGlobalTauri": true
```

**问题**: 启用 `withGlobalTauri` 使得前端可以通过 `window.__TAURI__` 全局访问 Tauri API，这意味着任何加载在页面上的第三方脚本（包括 npm 依赖、CDN 资源）都可以调用后端命令。

**修复建议**:
- 设置为 `false`，使用 `@tauri-apps/api` 的 ES module import 方式
- 如果必须启用，确保不使用 `unsafe-eval` 的 CSP 策略，并对所有第三方依赖进行审计

---

### 2.8 MEDIUM -- `read_local_file` 允许读取任意文件

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/fs/mod.rs` (第 337-347 行)

```rust
#[tauri::command]
pub async fn read_local_file(path: String) -&gt; Result&lt;FileContent, String&gt; {
    let raw = std::path::Path::new(&amp;path);
    let canonical = raw.canonicalize()...;
    let content = std::fs::read_to_string(&amp;canonical)...;
    Ok(FileContent { name, content })
}
```

**问题**: 该命令接受任意绝对路径，虽然使用了 `canonicalize()` 防止 `..` 遍历，但没有任何限制 -- 前端可以读取 `/etc/passwd`、`~/.ssh/id_rsa`、`~/.aws/credentials` 等敏感文件。

**修复建议**:
- 限制可读路径到用户显式打开的项目目录内
- 使用白名单机制，只允许读取 `.ab` 项目文件及相关工作区文件
- 考虑使用 `tauri-plugin-fs` 的 scope 限制，而非自定义命令

---

### 2.9 MEDIUM -- `db_execute_raw` 缺少 SQL 注入防护

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/db/mod.rs` (第 221-225 行)

```rust
#[tauri::command]
pub async fn db_execute_raw(sql: String, db_type: String) -&gt; Result&lt;QueryResult, String&gt; {
    dispatch_db!(db_type, execute_raw, &amp;sql)
}
```

**问题**: 这个命令直接执行原始 SQL，没有任何验证（与 `db_find_all` 等不同，后者有 `validate_identifier`）。业务流初始化（`bf_init`）使用 `include_str!` 读取迁移 SQL 并通过此命令执行，这虽然是可信代码路径，但前端也可以调用它。

**修复建议**: (与 2.2 联动) 移除该 command 注册，将迁移改为仅在 `setup()` 中自动执行。

---

### 2.10 MEDIUM -- `load_http_config` 错误处理吞没异常

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/lib.rs` (第 31-44 行)

```rust
fn load_http_config() -&gt; server::HttpConfig {
    match std::fs::read_to_string(&amp;path) {
        Ok(content) =&gt; serde_json::from_str::&lt;serde_json::Value&gt;(&amp;content)
            .ok()
            .and_then(|v| v.get("httpServer").cloned())
            .and_then(|hs| serde_json::from_value::&lt;server::HttpConfig&gt;(hs).ok())
            .unwrap_or_default(),
        Err(_) =&gt; server::HttpConfig::default(),
    }
}
```

**问题**: 任何解析错误都被静默吞没，回退到 `Default`（enabled: true）。这意味着一个格式错误的 settings.json 会悄无声息地启用 HTTP server。

**修复建议**: 至少记录一个 warning 日志：
```rust
Err(e) =&gt; {
    eprintln!("[ArchBot] Failed to read settings.json: {e}, using defaults");
    server::HttpConfig::default()
}
```

---

### 2.11 LOW -- 模块组织：`handlers/` 与领域模块并存

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/lib.rs`

**问题**: `lib.rs` 的 `invoke_handler` 注册了来自 `fs::`, `db::`, `data_standard::` 等**领域模块**的命令，同时也注册了来自 `handlers/` 的命令。但 `handlers/` 目录下的文件实现的是 Axum HTTP 路由，不是 Tauri command。这造成混淆：
- `handlers/` = Axum HTTP handlers（不是 Tauri commands）
- 真正的 Tauri commands 分布在各领域模块中（`fs/mod.rs`, `db/mod.rs`, `context.rs` 等）

**修复建议**: 将 `handlers/` 重命名为 `http/` 或 `api/`，明确其用途。

---

### 2.12 LOW -- 重复的 `now_iso()` 函数

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/lib.rs` (第 23-25 行) 和 `src-tauri/src/fs/mod.rs` (第 165-167 行)

**问题**: 两个位置定义了相同签名的 `now_iso()` 函数。`lib.rs` 的版本标记为 `pub(crate)`；`fs/mod.rs` 的版本是私有的。可能在编译时存在混淆。

**修复建议**: 统一使用 `lib.rs` 的 `pub(crate) fn now_iso()`，删除 `fs/mod.rs` 中的重复定义。

---

### 2.13 LOW -- `Cargo.toml` 中的 `crate-type` 冗余

**文件**: `src-tauri/Cargo.toml` (第 15 行)

```toml
crate-type = ["staticlib", "cdylib", "rlib"]
```

**问题**: 对于 Tauri 2 应用，通常只需要 `["staticlib", "cdylib", "rlib"]`。`rlib` 对桌面应用无实际作用，`staticlib` 主要用于移动端。

**修复建议**: 使用 Tauri 2 推荐的默认值（不显式指定 `crate-type`），或使用 `["staticlib", "cdylib", "rlib"]` 保持与 Tauri 2 模板一致。

---

### 2.14 LOW -- HTTP Server 默认启用

**文件**: `src-tauri/src/server.rs` (第 17-19 行)

```rust
fn default_enabled() -&gt; bool { true }
```

**问题**: Cargo.toml 中没有 `http` feature flag，HTTP server 始终编译并默认启用。对于不需要 HTTP API 的用户，这是不必要的攻击面和资源开销。

**修复建议**: 添加 `http-server` feature flag（默认关闭），让用户选择启用。

---

### 2.15 LOW -- `tauri::command` 未使用 `rename_all` 属性

**文件**: 各 handler 文件中的 `#[derive(Deserialize)]` 结构体

**问题**: 部分结构体使用 `#[serde(rename_all = "camelCase")]`（如 `db::QueryParams`），但许多 handler 的请求体没有显式声明 rename_all，依赖默认的 snake_case 规则。Vue 前端通常使用 camelCase 传递数据，可能导致序列化不匹配。

**修复建议**: 统一所有请求体的 `rename_all = "camelCase"`。

---

## 3. 架构模式总结

### 3.1 做得好 (Compliant)

| 维度 | 评价 |
|------|------|
| `#[tauri::command]` 注册 | **正确** -- 所有 command 均使用 `#[tauri::command]` 属性宏，通过 `generate_handler!` 集中注册 |
| Plugin 初始化 | **正确** -- `tauri-plugin-opener`, `tauri-plugin-dialog`, `tauri-plugin-fs` 在 builder 中正确注册 |
| `setup()` hook | **正确** -- 用于初始化 trace 系统 |
| `main.rs` 入口 | **正确** -- `#![windows_subsystem]` + 委托给 `lib.rs::run()` |
| `canonicalize()` 路径防护 | **正确** -- `LocalFs::resolve()` 使用 canonicalize + starts_with 防路径穿越 |
| SSRF 防护 | **正确** -- `RemoteFs::url()` 校验 host 一致性；`fetch_remote()` 禁止重定向和内网地址 |
| SQL 标识符校验 | **正确** -- `db::validate_identifier()` 对表名/字段名做严格校验 |
| Secret 加密存储 | **正确** -- `SecretManager` 使用 AES-256-GCM，机器 ID 派生密钥，文件权限 600 |
| 乐观锁 | **正确** -- `bf_update_flow` 实现 version-based optimistic locking |
| 业务流隔离 | **正确** -- `db_execute_raw` 已从 HTTP API 排除（有注释说明安全考虑） |

### 3.2 需要改进

| 维度 | 评价 |
|------|------|
| State 管理 | 应迁移到 `tauri::State&lt;T&gt;` + `app.manage()` |
| Capabilities 配置 | 缺少 `src-tauri/capabilities/` 目录 |
| CSP 策略 | 当前为 null（完全禁用） |
| HTTP API 安全 | 无认证机制 |
| 全局变量 | 6 处 `static OnceLock`，增加了测试难度 |

---

## 4. 建议的修复优先级

### 立即修复 (本周)

1. **CSP 配置**: 在 `tauri.conf.json` 中添加最小 CSP 策略
2. **移除 `db_execute_raw` command**: 改为自动执行迁移，不暴露给前端
3. **创建 capabilities 文件**: 声明所有 plugin 权限

### 近期修复 (本月)

4. **State 迁移**: 将 `OnceLock` 全局变量迁移到 `tauri::State`
5. **HTTP API 认证**: 添加 Bearer token 验证
6. **硬件指纹**: 使用 `mac_address` crate 替代 shell 命令
7. **`read_local_file` 路径限制**: 添加白名单或 scope 限制

### 持续改进

8. **模块重组**: `handlers/` 重命名为 `http/`
9. **Feature flags**: 为 HTTP server 添加可选 feature
10. **代码去重**: 移除重复的 `now_iso()`</result>

# ArchBot Rust/TypeScript Boundary Audit Report (ADR-001)

**Date:** 2026-06-07
**Principle:** Rust = System Capability Layer (thin, no business logic); TypeScript = Business Logic Layer
**Files Audited:** 21 Rust files / 10 TypeScript files

---

## BLOCKER (1 finding)

### BLOCKER-01: `business_flow/conductor.rs` -- Entire DAG Execution Engine in Rust

**File:** `src-tauri/src/business_flow/conductor.rs`
**Size:** 682 lines
**Severity:** BLOCKER

This file implements a complete multi-agent DAG execution engine in Rust, including topological sort, gateway strategy, condition evaluation, and degradation chains -- all of which ADR-001 explicitly assigns to TypeScript.

| Lines | Function / Block | Violation |
|-------|-----------------|-----------|
| 37--76 | `FlowGraph`, `FlowNode`, `FlowEdge`, `QualityGateConfig` structs | Duplicate types (these exist in `src/types/businessFlow.ts` as well). Graph structural types belong in TS alongside the flow designer UI. |
| 104--261 | `run_flow()` | Entire DAG execution orchestration: parses JSON graph, builds adjacency maps, traverses nodes, dispatches execution. **This is the core orchestrator and must move to TypeScript.** |
| 115 | `build_dag(&amp;graph)` call | DAG construction from edge list. ADR-001 says: "DAG 解析、拓扑排序 -&gt; 应在 TypeScript." |
| 118--123 | Start node detection | Business rule: "flow must have at least one Start node". |
| 131 | `topological_sort(...)` | **Explicit ADR-001 violation.** Topological sort is graph algorithm = business logic = TS. |
| 149--210 | AND gateway (parallel fork with `tokio::spawn` + `Semaphore`) | Gateway strategy explicitly belongs in TS. ADR-001: "网关策略（AND/XOR/OR 分叉） -&gt; 应在 TypeScript." |
| 211--238 | XOR gateway (conditional path selection) | Same gateway violation. |
| 244 | `apply_degradation(node)` call | ADR-001: "降级链策略 -&gt; 应在 TypeScript." |
| 265--291 | `execute_single_node()` dispatcher | Business logic: node type routing (start/end/agent/quality_gate/timer/sub_flow). |
| 295--388 | `execute_pass_through`, `execute_agent`, `execute_quality_gate`, `execute_timer`, `execute_sub_flow` | Node execution semantics. While agent execution ultimately spawns processes (system concern), the orchestration of *which* node executor to call and *what* parameters to pass is business logic. |
| 392--418 | `build_dag()` | Graph algorithm in Rust -- clear ADR-001 violation. |
| 420--459 | `topological_sort()` | Graph algorithm in Rust -- clear ADR-001 violation. |
| 463--475 | `evaluate_condition()` | Condition evaluation for XOR/OR gateways is business logic. |
| 479--502 | `apply_degradation()` | **Explicit ADR-001 violation.** Degradation chain strategy (warn -&gt; restart -&gt; skip -&gt; terminate) is business logic. |

**Repair plan:**
1. Move graph types (`FlowGraph`, `FlowNode`, `FlowEdge`) to a shared types package or delete the Rust duplicates (TS already has them in `src/types/businessFlow.ts`).
2. Move `build_dag()`, `topological_sort()`, `evaluate_condition()`, and `apply_degradation()` to a new `src/orchestration/DagEngine.ts`.
3. Move gateway dispatching (AND/XOR/OR) to `DagEngine.ts`.
4. Move node-type routing to `DagEngine.ts`.
5. Rust should only retain: `start_flow_run()` (Tauri command entry point), process spawning per agent node, Tauri event emission (`emit_event`). The `bf_run_flow` and `bf_abort_run` Tauri commands should become thin wrappers that receive an execution plan from TypeScript.

---

## HIGH (1 finding)

### HIGH-01: `business_flow/validation.rs` -- Graph Structural Validation in Rust

**File:** `src-tauri/src/business_flow/validation.rs`
**Size:** 299 lines
**Severity:** HIGH

ADR-001 states: "图合法性校验（Start/End/连通性） -&gt; 应在 TypeScript（Zod）". This entire file is graph structural validation.

| Lines | Function | Violation |
|-------|----------|-----------|
| 41--134 | `validate_flow()` | Core validation orchestrator checking: Start node count (lines 60--74), End node count (lines 77--83), orphan edges (lines 87--103), disconnected nodes (lines 107--121), cycles (lines 124--131). All are business-level structural rules. |
| 137--165 | `build_adjacency_map()` + `bfs_reachable()` | Graph BFS for connectivity check -- algorithm belongs in TS. |
| 167--208 | `detect_cycle()` + `dfs_cycle()` | DFS-based cycle detection -- algorithm belongs in TS. |

Note: `validation.rs` has its own `FlowGraph` / `NodeEntry` / `EdgeEntry` types (lines 17--36) that are a subset of the graph types -- further duplication with both `conductor.rs` and `src/types/businessFlow.ts`.

**Repair plan:**
1. Define Zod schemas in TypeScript for flow graph validation at `src/orchestration/FlowGraphValidator.ts`.
2. Implement `validateFlow(graph)` in TypeScript with the same checks (Start/End count, orphan edges, BFS reachability, DFS cycle detection).
3. Rust `bf_validate_flow` and `bf_validate_graph` commands should become thin pass-through wrappers that deserialize JSON and call into the TS validation (or the TS side should validate before persisting, avoiding the round-trip entirely).
4. The existing Rust tests (lines 211--298) should be ported to Vitest tests in TypeScript.

---

## MEDIUM (4 findings)

### MEDIUM-01: `business_flow/handler.rs` -- Business Rules Mixed into CRUD

**File:** `src-tauri/src/business_flow/handler.rs`
**Severity:** MEDIUM

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 139--144 | `if existing.published { return Err("Cannot modify a published flow. Copy it first.") }` and `if existing.flow_type == "builtin" { return Err("...") }` | Business rules about workflow state. Published/built-in immutability is a product decision, not a data integrity concern. |
| 174--176 | `if existing.flow_type == "builtin" { return Err("Built-in flows cannot be deleted") }` | Same pattern -- business rule. |
| 239 | `format!("{} (Copy)", existing.name)` | Naming convention for copied flows -- business logic. |
| 132--137 | Optimistic locking version check | Borderline: could argue this is data integrity (DB concern), but it is enforced in the handler rather than the DB layer. Acceptable to keep. |
| 178--203 | Cascade delete logic (artifacts -&gt; runs -&gt; flow) | Data integrity/DB concern, but the ordering and inclusion/exclusion logic is borderline business logic. Acceptable to keep as a DB concern. |

**Repair plan:**
1. Move published/builtin immutability checks to TypeScript (in `flowStore.ts` before calling `bf_update_flow` or `bf_delete_flow`).
2. Move "(Copy)" naming to TypeScript.
3. Keep optimistic locking and cascade delete in Rust as data integrity concerns.

### MEDIUM-02: `ai_config.rs` -- Hardcoded Provider Configuration in Rust

**File:** `src-tauri/src/ai_config.rs`
**Severity:** MEDIUM

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 35--145 | `builtin_providers()` function | 110 lines of hardcoded AI provider definitions (9 providers, each with name, protocol, base_url, models list, default_model). This is **configuration/policy data** that ADR-001 says belongs in TypeScript (like `src/config/scenarios.ts` or `src/config/menus.yml`). |
| 160--188 | `load_providers_raw()` merge logic | The merge strategy (saved providers + missing built-ins) is borderline configuration management logic. |

The SSRF protection (lines 314--384), HTTP validation (lines 387--542), and provider secret management (lines 304--307) are correctly in Rust.

**Repair plan:**
1. Move the builtin provider list to a TypeScript config file (e.g., `src/config/aiProviders.ts` or `ai-providers.yml` loaded by `ConfigLoader`).
2. Keep `load_providers_raw()` as a file I/O function that reads/writes the YAML file. The merge with built-ins would then happen in TypeScript.
3. The `ai_validate_provider` command (HTTP connectivity test) correctly stays in Rust.

### MEDIUM-03: `agent_runtime/session_manager.rs` -- State Machine and Cache Policy in Rust

**File:** `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/session_manager.rs`
**Severity:** MEDIUM

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 314--326 | `update_status()` state machine validation: `match (session.status.as_str(), new_status)` with valid transitions | ADR-001 says state machines belong in TypeScript. This is a classic finite state machine (active/paused/closed/archived) implemented as a Rust match statement. |
| 134--137 | In-memory store trimming: `if store.len() &gt; 1000 { ... keep last 500 }` | Cache eviction policy is a configuration/strategy decision, borderline business logic. |

The DB CRUD operations (lines 103--128, 226--304, 429--581) are correctly in Rust.

**Repair plan:**
1. Move the state machine to a TypeScript utility (e.g., `src/orchestration/SessionStateMachine.ts`) that validates transitions before calling `agent_update_session_status`.
2. The cache trimming threshold (1000/500) could become a configuration constant managed by TypeScript.

### MEDIUM-04: `agent_runtime/context_assembly.rs` -- Hardcoded Execution Policies in Rust

**File:** `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/context_assembly.rs`
**Severity:** MEDIUM

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 78--83 | `select_window()` sliding window algorithm | Context management strategy (how many recent messages to include) is prompt engineering / business logic. |
| 87--109 | `compress_history()` | History compression strategy is prompt engineering logic. |
| 176--181 | `timeout_seconds: 1800`, `allow_file_write: true`, `allow_shell: false` | Hardcoded execution policy values. These are configuration that should come from TypeScript. |
| 112--197 | `assemble_turn_input()` | YAML assembly with fixed templates -- this is prompt engineering logic. |

**Repair plan:**
1. Move the sliding window size (10) to a TypeScript-managed configuration constant.
2. Move execution policy defaults (timeout, file_write, shell) to TypeScript config.
3. Keep `assemble_turn_input()` as a data formatting utility in Rust (it assembles a YAML blob for the agent runtime), but have it accept policy values as parameters from TypeScript rather than hardcoding them.

---

## LOW (5 findings)

### LOW-01: `data_standard.rs` -- Hardcoded Default Conventions

**File:** `src-tauri/src/data_standard.rs`
**Severity:** LOW

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 158--170 | Default conventions: `table_prefix: "t_"`, `field_naming: "snake_case"`, `primary_key: "id (bigint, auto_increment)"`, audit fields list, soft delete | These are domain-level defaults that could be managed by TypeScript configuration, but they are essentially file-level default initialization for YAML-based storage. Minor concern. |

**Repair plan:** Consider moving defaults to a TypeScript config constant that is passed to `ds_create_domain`. Not urgent.

### LOW-02: `agent_runtime/turn_executor.rs` -- URL Derivation Logic

**File:** `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/turn_executor.rs`
**Severity:** LOW

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 150--174 | ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL derivation from AI provider config (base URL conversion logic) | This is configuration derivation logic. Borderline -- the URL conversion is a system-level detail needed for process spawning. |
| 176--187 | Model override logic (key selection per runtime type) | Configuration/env name mapping. Borderline. |
| 590--777 | `generate_input_yml()`, `build_stdin_prompt()` | Prompt/input assembly for agent runtime. The template content (expected_output: "根据用户指令分析代码并输出结果") is hardcoded Chinese text that should come from config. |

**Repair plan:** 
1. Move URL derivation to a utility that takes a config object. Could stay in Rust as it's needed for process launch.
2. Move prompt templates to TypeScript config (i18n-aware).

### LOW-03: `agent_runtime/shell_control.rs` -- Default Blocked Commands List

**File:** `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/shell_control.rs`
**Severity:** LOW

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 7--29 | `default_blocked_commands()` with 15 commands | Security policy list. Could be managed in TS config but reasonable to keep in Rust as a security baseline. |
| 31--45 | `default_blocked_patterns()` with 10 patterns | Same as above. |

**Repair plan:** Not urgent. The blocked commands list is a security baseline that is reasonable to keep in Rust. The `CommandGuard` runtime (lines 49--176) is correctly a system concern.

### LOW-04: `agent_runtime/agent_config_handler.rs` -- Configuration Wiring

**File:** `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/agent_config_handler.rs`
**Severity:** LOW

| Lines | Code | Violation |
|-------|------|-----------|
| 101--149 | `agent_get_status()` config assembly | Reads runtimes.yml and assembles config info. Mostly I/O + data reshaping, acceptable. |
| 180--262 | `agent_save_config()` | Writes to runtimes.yml. The URL conversion logic (lines 204--214) is duplicated from turn_executor. |

**Repair plan:** Acceptable as configuration persistence. The URL conversion logic could be centralized into a shared utility to eliminate the duplication with `turn_executor.rs`.

### LOW-05: `scenario.rs`, `context.rs` -- Clean

**Files:** `src-tauri/src/scenario.rs`, `src-tauri/src/context.rs`
**Severity:** N/A (no violations)

Both files are pure file I/O wrappers: read/write YAML files from the project filesystem. The scenario strategy definitions are correctly in `src/config/scenarios.ts` (TypeScript). No violations.

---

## Summary Table

| # | Severity | File | Lines | Issue |
|---|----------|------|-------|-------|
| B-01 | **BLOCKER** | `business_flow/conductor.rs` | 1--682 | Entire DAG engine: topo sort, gateway dispatch, condition eval, degradation chain |
| H-01 | **HIGH** | `business_flow/validation.rs` | 1--299 | Graph validation: cycle detection, BFS connectivity, Start/End checks |
| M-01 | MEDIUM | `business_flow/handler.rs` | 139--176, 239 | Business rules: published/builtin immutability, "(Copy)" naming |
| M-02 | MEDIUM | `ai_config.rs` | 35--145 | 110 lines of hardcoded provider definitions |
| M-03 | MEDIUM | `agent_runtime/session_manager.rs` | 314--326, 134--137 | State machine validation, cache trimming policy |
| M-04 | MEDIUM | `agent_runtime/context_assembly.rs` | 78--109, 176--181 | Sliding window algorithm, hardcoded execution policies |
| L-01 | LOW | `data_standard.rs` | 158--170 | Default conventions as hardcoded values |
| L-02 | LOW | `agent_runtime/turn_executor.rs` | 150--174, 590--777 | URL derivation, hardcoded prompt templates |
| L-03 | LOW | `agent_runtime/shell_control.rs` | 7--45 | Default blocked commands list |
| L-04 | LOW | `agent_runtime/agent_config_handler.rs` | 101--149 | Configuration assembly (acceptable) |

## Files That Correctly Follow ADR-001

These Rust files are clean -- they perform only system capabilities (file I/O, DB operations, process management):

- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/version_manager.rs` -- Executable detection, version management, symlinks
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/skill_installer.rs` -- Git clone for skill installation
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/file_control.rs` -- File snapshots, git diff, rollback
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/launcher.rs` -- Process spawning
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/home_setup.rs` -- Isolated HOME directory setup
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/event_stream.rs` -- SSE event bus
- `src-tauri/src/agent_runtime/audit.rs` -- File access audit logging
- `src-tauri/src/scenario.rs` -- YAML file read/write for scenario config
- `src-tauri/src/context.rs` -- YAML file read/write for context entries
- `src-tauri/src/db/` -- SQLite CRUD dispatch layer
- `src-tauri/src/fs/` -- File system operations
- `src-tauri/src/handlers/*_handler.rs` -- HTTP route wiring (thin pass-through)

These TypeScript files are correctly positioned as the business logic layer:

| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `src/orchestration/ConfigLoader.ts` | YML config loading with Zod validation and fallback |
| `src/orchestration/ConfigValidator.ts` | Zod schemas for all config types |
| `src/orchestration/FlowExecutor.ts` | Multi-step flow execution engine |
| `src/orchestration/ActionRegistry.ts` | Action handler registry |
| `src/orchestration/ContextMenuResolver.ts` | Menu resolution with dynamic provider registration |
| `src/orchestration/ExpressionEvaluator.ts` | Custom boolean expression parser |
| `src/orchestration/ParameterResolver.ts` | Template parameter resolution |
| `src/orchestration/PredicateRegistry.ts` | Named predicate registry |
| `src/orchestration/RuntimeContext.ts` | Runtime state aggregation |
| `src/types/businessFlow.ts` | Full TypeScript type definitions for flow domain |
| `src/stores/flowStore.ts` | Flow state management with IPC wrappers |
| `src/composables/useBusinessFlow.ts` | Reactive computed properties on flow state |
| `src/config/scenarios.ts` | Scenario preset definitions |
| `src/config/menu.ts` | Menu configuration (deprecated in favor of YML) |

## Recommended Relocation Priority

1. **Immediate (BLOCKER):** Move `business_flow/conductor.rs` DAG engine to TypeScript. This is ~500 lines of core business logic that should live in `src/orchestration/DagEngine.ts`. The Rust side should be reduced to a thin process-spawning layer (~100 lines).

2. **Next sprint (HIGH):** Move `business_flow/validation.rs` to TypeScript as `src/orchestration/FlowGraphValidator.ts`. The Rust command should become a simple pass-through or be removed entirely (TS validates before persistence).

3. **Within 2 sprints (MEDIUM):** Move business rules out of `handler.rs`, relocate builtin provider config from `ai_config.rs`, extract state machine from `session_manager.rs`.

4. **Backlog (LOW):** Move defaults from `data_standard.rs`, extract prompt templates from `turn_executor.rs`, centralize URL derivation logic.</result>

/// Update the status of a flow run from TypeScript.
/// Called by the TS-side DagEngine during execution.
#[tauri::command]
pub async fn bf_update_run_status(
    run_id: String,
    status: String,
    error_message: Option<String>,
) -> Result<(), String> {
    update_run_status(&run_id, &status, error_message.as_deref()).await
}

## ArchBot Business Flow Editor -- Full Analysis

---

### 1. How Many Node Types Are Currently in the Palette?

There are **8 palette entries** in `paletteItems` (lines 85-94 of `BusinessFlowEditorPanel.vue`):

| Palette Index | `type` key       | Vue Flow `nodeTypes` key | Component              |
|---------------|------------------|---------------------------|------------------------|
| 1             | `start`          | `start`                   | `StartNode.vue`        |
| 2             | `end`            | `end`                     | `EndNode.vue`          |
| 3             | `agent`          | `agent`                   | `AgentNode.vue`        |
| 4             | `gateway_xor`    | `gateway_xor`             | `GatewayNode.vue`      |
| 5             | `gateway_and`    | `gateway_and`             | `GatewayNode.vue`      |
| 6             | `gateway_or`     | `gateway_or`              | `GatewayNode.vue`      |
| 7             | `material_input` | `material_input`          | `MaterialInputNode.vue`|
| 8             | `quality_gate`   | `quality_gate`            | `QualityGateNode.vue`  |

However, the `NodeType` union in `/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/types/businessFlow.ts` (line 10-27) defines **13 values**:

- **P0 (6):** `start`, `end`, `agent`, `gateway_xor`, `gateway_and`, `gateway_or`
- **P1 (3):** `material_input`, `quality_gate`, `sub_flow`
- **P2 (4):** `timer`, `signal`, `error_handler`, `human_approval`

So **5 types are defined but not in the palette**: `sub_flow`, `timer`, `signal`, `error_handler`, `human_approval`. They have no Vue Flow component registration, no palette entry, and no `getDefaultNodeData` case -- but the `DagEngine` does handle all of them in its `executeNode` switch.

---

### 2. Palette UI Structure (HTML/CSS)

Located at lines 356-379 of `BusinessFlowEditorPanel.vue`:

```html
&lt;!-- Left toolbar: palette --&gt;
&lt;div v-if="!readOnly"
     class="w-[160px] shrink-0 border-r border-border-default
            bg-surface-50 dark:bg-surface-50 overflow-y-auto"&gt;
  &lt;div class="p-2"&gt;
    &lt;p class="text-[10px] font-semibold uppercase text-text-muted mb-2 tracking-wider"&gt;
      &lt;!-- i18n label for "Flow Controls" --&gt;
    &lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;div class="flex flex-col gap-1"&gt;
      &lt;div v-for="item in paletteItems" :key="item.type"
           class="flex items-center gap-2 px-2 py-1.5 rounded-md
                  text-xs text-text-primary
                  hover:bg-surface-100 dark:hover:bg-surface-200
                  cursor-grab select-none transition-colors"
           draggable="true"
           @dragstart="onDragStart($event, item.type)"&gt;
        &lt;span class="text-base w-5 text-center"&gt;{{ item.icon }}&lt;/span&gt;
        &lt;span class="truncate"&gt;{{ item.label }}&lt;/span&gt;
      &lt;/div&gt;
    &lt;/div&gt;
  &lt;/div&gt;
&lt;/div&gt;
```

Key structural points:
- Fixed **160px width**, left sidebar
- Hidden when `readOnly` (published or builtin flow)
- Uses **native HTML drag-and-drop** (`draggable="true"`, `@dragstart`)
- Each item is a flex row: emoji icon (20px fixed width) + i18n label
- Tailwind utility classes: `cursor-grab`, hover highlight, rounded corners, 2px padding

---

### 3. How Drag-and-Drop Works (Palette to Canvas)

The DnD flow uses 3 handlers on `BusinessFlowEditorPanel.vue`:

1. **`onDragStart`** (line 100-104): Sets the node type string as `application/vueflow` MIME data on the drag event.

2. **`onDragOver`** (line 106-114): Calls `event.preventDefault()` -- this is mandatory for the browser to allow a drop.

3. **`onDrop`** (line 118-139): Reads the MIME type, converts screen coordinates to flow coordinates via `screenToFlowCoordinate()`, creates a new `Node` with a timestamp-based ID, calls `addNodes([newNode])` to route through Vue Flow's internal change pipeline, and sets `dirty = true`.

Both `@dragover` and `@drop` are placed directly on the `&lt;VueFlow&gt;` element (line 397-398), which is the official Vue Flow pattern.

---

### 4. How Custom Vue Flow Nodes Are Registered

At lines 66-75 of `BusinessFlowEditorPanel.vue`:

```typescript
const nodeTypes: Record&lt;string, any&gt; = {
  start: markRaw(StartNode),
  end: markRaw(EndNode),
  agent: markRaw(AgentNode),
  gateway_xor: markRaw(GatewayNode),
  gateway_and: markRaw(GatewayNode),
  gateway_or: markRaw(GatewayNode),
  material_input: markRaw(MaterialInputNode),
  quality_gate: markRaw(QualityGateNode),
}
```

This map is passed as `:node-types="nodeTypes"` to the `&lt;VueFlow&gt;` component (line 390). Each key is the string that Vue Flow uses to look up the component when rendering a node whose `type` field matches. `markRaw()` prevents Vue from making the component objects reactive (a Vue Flow performance best practice).

All three gateway types (`gateway_xor`, `gateway_and`, `gateway_or`) share the same `GatewayNode.vue` component, which uses the `type` prop (passed by Vue Flow automatically) to compute the diamond symbol and border color at render time.

---

### 5. Individual Node .vue Files

| File | Node Type(s) | Props | Handles | Visual |
|------|-------------|-------|---------|--------|
| **StartNode.vue** | `start` | `data: { label }` | Source (Bottom) | Green circle, 48x48 |
| **EndNode.vue** | `end` | `data: { label }` | Target (Top) | Red circle, 48x48 |
| **AgentNode.vue** | `agent` | `data: { agentName?, skillName?, label? }` | Target (Top) + Source (Bottom) | Blue-bordered rounded rectangle, emoji icon + agent name + skill name |
| **GatewayNode.vue** | `gateway_xor`, `gateway_and`, `gateway_or` | `data: { label? }`, plus `type` (Vue Flow injected) | Target (Top) + Source (Bottom), both counter-rotated | 56x56 diamond (rotate-45), symbol/border color by type (amber/purple/cyan) |
| **MaterialInputNode.vue** | `material_input` | `data: { label?, fileName?, filePath?, fileType? }` | Source only (Bottom) | Emerald-bordered rounded rectangle, file emoji + filename + extension |
| **QualityGateNode.vue** | `quality_gate` | `data: { label?, metric?, threshold? }` | Target (Top) + Source (Bottom) | Orange-bordered rounded rectangle, shield emoji + "metric &gt;= threshold" |

---

### 6. DagEngine.executeNode Switch Statement

Located at lines 224-249 of `/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/orchestration/DagEngine.ts`. It handles **all 12 node types** plus a `default` fallback:

| Case | Executor Function | Behavior |
|------|-------------------|----------|
| `start`, `end`, `material_input`, `signal`, `error_handler` | `executePassThrough()` | Always returns success, no-op |
| `agent` | `executeAgentNode()` | Calls Rust `agent_execute_turn` via IPC |
| `quality_gate` | `executeQualityGate()` | Always passes (MVP stub) |
| `timer` | `executeTimer()` | `setTimeout` for configured duration |
| `sub_flow` | `executeSubFlow()` | Recursively instantiates a new `DagEngine`, parses sub-flow JSON, executes it |
| `human_approval` | `executeHumanApproval()` | Calls `runtime.confirm()` for user dialog |
| `default` | `executePassThrough()` | Safety net for unknown types |

**Gateway types** (`gateway_xor`, `gateway_and`, `gateway_or`) are NOT in the `executeNode` switch because they are handled at the **topological traversal level** (lines 118-179 of `DagEngine.ts`) -- they control which downstream nodes execute and in what order, rather than being executed themselves.

---

### 7. What Is Missing vs. 18 Roles / Numeric Gates / Skill Nodes / Reference Nodes

**18 Roles:** The type system has only one agent-like node (`agent`), which stores `agentId`, `agentName`, and `skillName`. There is no concept of 18 distinct role types (e.g., Architect, Reviewer, Coder, Tester, etc.). Each role would likely need its own `NodeType` value (or a single `role` type with a `roleName` discriminator), its own Vue Flow component, palette entry, `NodeData` interface, and `DagEngine` executor.

**Numeric Gates:** The existing gateways are purely logical (XOR/AND/OR). There is no numeric gateway type (e.g., "gateway_numeric" that evaluates threshold expressions like `coverage &gt; 80%` or `responseTime &lt; 500ms`). This would be distinct from `quality_gate` (which is a pass-through node, not a routing decision point).

**Skill Nodes:** Skills are currently a *property* of the `AgentNode` (`skillName` field), not a standalone node type. A dedicated skill node would be a first-class flow element that can be independently connected, configured, and reused.

**Reference Nodes:** No reference node type exists -- nothing that represents a cross-reference to external documentation, another flow, a code entity, or a knowledge base article.

---

### 8. Where New Node Types Would Need to Be Added

For each new node type, changes are required in these files:

1. **`/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/types/businessFlow.ts`**
   - Add the new value to the `NodeType` union (line 11-27)
   - Add a new `*NodeData` interface (e.g., `SkillNodeData`, `NumericGatewayNodeData`)
   - Add it to the `NodeData` union (line 113-124)

2. **`/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/components/domain/business-flow/nodes/`**
   - Create a new `.vue` component (e.g., `SkillNode.vue`, `NumericGatewayNode.vue`)
   - Must import `Handle` and `Position` from `@vue-flow/core`
   - Must declare props for `data` matching the NodeData interface
   - Must use `Handle` components for connection points

3. **`/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/components/domain/business-flow/BusinessFlowEditorPanel.vue`** (4 insertion points)
   - Import the new `.vue` component (around line 26-31)
   - Add it to the `nodeTypes` map wrapped in `markRaw()` (line 66-75)
   - Add a `PaletteItem` entry to `paletteItems` (line 85-94)
   - Add a `case` in `getDefaultNodeData()` (line 141-162)

4. **`/Users/baodan/RustroverProjects/ArchBot/src/orchestration/DagEngine.ts`**
   - Add a `case` in the `executeNode()` switch (line 224-249)
   - Implement the executor function (e.g., `executeSkillNode()`, `executeNumericGateway()`)
   - For gateway-type nodes that affect routing, handle them in the topological traversal loop (around lines 118-179) rather than in `executeNode`

5. **i18n keys** -- Add translation keys for the new palette labels (referenced via `tt('businessFlow.editor.nodes.xxx')` on line 87).</result>

```typescript async function executeEmployeeNode(
  node: FlowNode,
  runtime: ActionRuntime,
  options: DagExecutionOptions,
): Promise<NodeResult> {
  const data = node.data as { employeeCode?: string; employeeName?: string; skillName?: string }
  const employeeCode = data.employeeCode ?? 'unknown'
  const employeeName = data.employeeName ?? 'Employee'

  try {
    await runtime.invoke('agent_execute_turn', {
      agentId: employeeCode,
      agentName: employeeName,
      skillName: data.skillName,
      materialPaths: options.materialPaths,
    })

    return {
      nodeId: node.id,
      success: true,
      message: `${employeeName} completed`,
      outputPath: `${options.outputDir}/${options.runId}/${node.id}`,
    }
  } catch (e: unknown) {
    const msg = e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e)
    return { nodeId: node.id, success: false, message: `${employeeName} failed: ${msg}` }
  }
}
